✓ active — 6 loci · 6 memory · 9 corpus
⚠ CorpusRegrades 'hop-sweep' sweeps 'hops', which requires multi-hop retrieval (see docs/SCC-MULTIHOP.md). Fusion reorders a packet; it cannot add a document retrieval never returned -- so a hop is a RETRIEVAL capability, not a fusion setting. If the SCC does not implement it, /configure IGNORES the field and every combo scores identically — an inert knob that looks exactly like a real ceiling. The regrade will hard-error unless the SCC advertises 'hops' in GET /stores.
